Analysis of the test files (`GroupCoordinatorServiceTest.java`, `GroupCoordinatorShardTest.java`, and `GroupMetadataManagerTest.java`) reveals several important failure modes and state transition scenarios that lack dedicated regression tests. These gaps expose the coordinator to potential data loss, incorrect partition assignments, resource leaks, and inconsistent group state transitions during error conditions.\n\n## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Member Epoch Transitions During Coordinator Unavailability\n\n- **Risk**: HIGH\n- **Code Location**: GroupCoordinatorService.java ~line 479-508 (consumerGroupHeartbeat method)\n- **Description**: When the coordinator is briefly unavailable (transitioning between leaders) and members continue sending heartbeats with incrementing epochs, the current tests only verify the COORDINATOR_NOT_AVAILABLE error response. However, there's no test ensuring that when the coordinator becomes available again, it correctly processes the accumulated epoch changes without skipping any transitions or duplicating assignments. This can lead to members being assigned to the same partition.\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testConsumerGroupHeartbeatEpochTransitionsAcrossCoordinatorFailover() throws ExecutionException, InterruptedException, TimeoutException {\n      GroupCoordinatorService service = new GroupCoordinatorServiceBuilder()\n          .setConfig(createConfig())\n          .setRuntime(mockRuntime())\n          .build();\n\n      String groupId = \"test-group\";\n      String memberId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n\n      // Service not started - coordinator unavailable\n      ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData request = new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .setMemberId(memberId)\n          .setMemberEpoch(0)\n          .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n          .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"topic-1\"))\n          .setTopicPartitions(List.of());\n\n      CompletableFuture<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData> future1 = service.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n          requestContext(ApiKeys.CONSUMER_GROUP_HEARTBEAT),\n          request\n      );\n\n      assertEquals(Errors.COORDINATOR_NOT_AVAILABLE.code(), future1.get(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS).errorCode());\n\n      // Start coordinator\n      service.start();\n\n      // Member sends heartbeat with epoch 1 (skipped epoch 0 transition)\n      request.setMemberEpoch(1);\n      CompletableFuture<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData> future2 = service.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n          requestContext(ApiKeys.CONSUMER_GROUP_HEARTBEAT),\n          request\n      );\n\n      // Verify the assignment contains this member (not another member)\n      ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData response = future2.get(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n      assertTrue(response.memberEpoch() >= 1, \"Member should have valid epoch after failover\");\n      assertNotEquals(Errors.FENCED_INSTANCE_ID.code(), response.errorCode());\n\n      service.shutdown();\n  }\n  ```\n- **Coverage Delta**: This test would exercise the `throwIfNotActive()` check at line 479, the state transition logic in GroupMetadataManager for member epoch validation, and the recovery path when the coordinator becomes active again. It hits critical paths in `GroupMetadataManager.consumerGroupHeartbeat()`.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Offset Expiration During Rebalance In Progress\n\n- **Risk**: HIGH\n- **Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java (offset expiration logic during group state transitions)\n- **Description**: Offsets can expire based on inactivity, but the existing tests (`GroupMetadataManagerTest`) don't verify that offset expiration is correctly skipped or handled when a group is in the REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS state. If offset expiration proceeds during rebalancing, committed offsets could be lost mid-rebalance, causing consumers to restart from the wrong position or lose progress entirely.\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testOffsetExpirationSkippedDuringRebalanceInProgress() throws Exception {\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n          .build();\n\n      String groupId = \"test-group\";\n      String memberId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n      String topicName = \"test-topic\";\n      Uuid topicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n\n      // Create consumer group and commit offsets\n      context.replay(\n          new ConsumerGroupMemberMetadataValue()\n              .setMemberId(memberId)\n              .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n      );\n\n      OffsetCommitRequestData offsetCommitRequest = new OffsetCommitRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .addTopic(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestTopic()\n              .setName(topicName)\n              .addPartition(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestPartition()\n                  .setPartitionIndex(0)\n                  .setCommittedOffset(100)\n                  .setCommitTimestamp(context.time.milliseconds())\n              )\n          );\n\n      context.groupMetadataManager.commitOffset(requestContext(), offsetCommitRequest);\n\n      // Trigger rebalance - group state becomes REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS\n      ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData heartbeatRequest = new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .setMemberId(memberId)\n          .setMemberEpoch(0)\n          .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n          .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n          .setTopicPartitions(List.of());\n\n      context.groupMetadataManager.consumerGroupHeartbeat(requestContext(), heartbeatRequest);\n\n      // Advance time beyond offset retention\n      context.time.sleep(context.offsetsRetentionMs + 1000);\n\n      // Offset should still exist because group is rebalancing\n      OffsetFetchRequestData fetchRequest = new OffsetFetchRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .addTopic(new OffsetFetchRequestData.OffsetFetchRequestTopic()\n              .setName(topicName)\n              .addPartition(0)\n          );\n\n      OffsetFetchResponseData fetchResponse = context.groupMetadataManager.fetchOffsets(requestContext(), fetchRequest);\n      assertEquals(100L, fetchResponse.topics().get(0).partitions().get(0).committedOffset());\n\n      context.close();\n  }\n  ```\n- **Coverage Delta**: This test exercises offset expiration logic in OffsetMetadataManager while the group is in REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS state. It validates the state machine's protection against premature offset deletion and hits the isOffsetExpired check in OffsetMetadataManager that considers group state.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Member Removal with Unresolved Assignments\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java (member removal logic), GroupCoordinatorShard.java (deleteGroups method ~line 269)\n- **Description**: When a member is removed from a group (via LeaveGroup or timeout), the current test coverage doesn't verify that partial or in-flight partition assignments are correctly cleaned up. If a member's target assignment record exists but hasn't been applied (current assignment not yet updated), removing the member without cleaning up the target assignment can cause the partition to remain unassigned or cause conflicts when another member joins.\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testMemberRemovalWithPendingTargetAssignment() throws Exception {\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n          .build();\n\n      String groupId = \"test-group\";\n      String memberId1 = .setGroupId(groupId)\n              .setState(ConsumerGroupState.STABLE.toString())\n      );\n\n      // Add first member with subscription\n      ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData joinRequest = new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .setMemberId(memberId1)\n          .setMemberEpoch(0)\n          .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n          .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n          .setTopicPartitions(List.of());\n\n      CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> joinResult =\n          context.groupMetadataManager.consumerGroupHeartbeat(requestContext(), joinRequest);\n\n      // Verify target assignment created\n      assertTrue(context.hasTargetAssignment(groupId, memberId1));\n\n      // Member leaves before current assignment is applied\n      LeaveGroupRequestData leaveRequest = new LeaveGroupRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .addMember(new context.groupMetadataManager.leaveGroup(requestContext(), leaveRequest);\n\n      // Verify all target assignments for the member are removed\n      assertFalse(context.hasTargetAssignment(groupId, memberId1),\n          \"Target assignment should be cleaned up when member leaves\");\n\n      // Verify group can be deleted without issues\n      DeleteGroupsResponseData.DeletableGroupResultCollection deleteResult =\n          context.groupMetadataManager.deleteGroups(requestContext(), List.of(groupId));\n\n      assertEquals(Errors.NONE.code(), deleteResult.iterator().next().errorCode());\n\n      context.close();\n  }\n  ```\n- **Coverage Delta**: This test exercises the member removal path in GroupMetadataManager.leaveGroup() and validates cleanup of both current and target assignments. It hits the record generation logic that creates tombstone records for ConsumerGroupTargetAssignmentMemberValue.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Concurrent Offset Commits During Member Epoch Bump\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java (offset commit validation), OffsetMetadataManager.java (commitOffset method)\n- **Description**: When a member's epoch is bumped during rebalancing, a consumer might simultaneously attempt to commit offsets using its old epoch. The current tests don't verify that offset commits from members with outdated epochs are correctly rejected with FENCED_MEMBER_EPOCH, preventing the coordinator from accepting stale offsets. This can result in incorrect offset tracking if a consumer commits with a stale epoch before realizing it has been fenced.\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testOffsetCommitRejectedWhenMemberEpochBumped() throws Exception {\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n          .build();\n\n      String groupId = \"test-group\";\n      String memberId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n      String topicName = \"test-topic\";\n\n      // Member joins group and receives epoch 1\n      ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData joinRequest = new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .setMemberId(memberId)\n          .setMemberEpoch(0)\n          .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n          .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n          .setTopicPartitions(List.of());\n\n      CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> joinResult =\n          context.groupMetadataManager.consumerGroupHeartbeat(requestContext(), joinRequest);\n\n      int firstEpoch = joinResult.response().memberEpoch();\n\n      // Member receives new epoch due to rebalance\n      ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData heartbeatRequest = new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .setMemberId(memberId)\n          .setMemberEpoch(firstEpoch)\n          .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n          .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n          .setTopicPartitions(List.of());\n\n      CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> rebalanceResult =\n          context.groupMetadataManager.consumerGroupHeartbeat(requestContext(), heartbeatRequest);\n\n      int newEpoch = rebalanceResult.response().memberEpoch();\n      assertTrue(newEpoch > firstEpoch, \"Member epoch should increase during rebalance\");\n\n      // Member attempts to commit offset with OLD epoch (race condition)\n      OffsetCommitRequestData offsetCommitRequest = new OffsetCommitRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .setMemberId(memberId)\n          .setGenerationIdOrMemberEpoch(firstEpoch)  // Using old epoch\n          .addTopic(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestTopic()\n              .setName(topicName)\n              .addPartition(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestPartition()\n                  .setPartitionIndex(0)\n                  .setCommittedOffset(100)\n              )\n          );\n\n      CoordinatorResult<OffsetCommitResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> commitResult =\n          context.groupMetadataManager.commitOffset(requestContext(), offsetCommitRequest);\n\n      // Should reject with FENCED_MEMBER_EPOCH\n      assertEquals(Errors.FENCED_MEMBER_EPOCH.code(),\n          commitResult.response().topics().get(0).partitions().get(0).errorCode());\n\n      context.close();\n  }\n  ```\n- **Coverage Delta**: This test exercises the member epoch validation in OffsetMetadataManager.commitOffset() at the point where it checks member epoch consistency. It validates the FENCED_MEMBER_EPOCH error path and ensures stale offset commits are rejected.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 5: Partition Assignment Completeness Check During Consumer Scaling\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java (target assignment generation and application), GroupCoordinatorShard.java (partition assignment logic)\n- **Description**: When consumers scale up/down, the partition assignment algorithm should cover all subscribed partitions. However, existing tests don't verify the scenario where the assignor returns an incomplete assignment (e.g., due to a bug or misconfiguration) that leaves some partitions unassigned. The coordinator should either reject this or handle it gracefully, but there's no test ensuring partitions aren't silently dropped from assignments.\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testPartitionAssignmentCompletenessValidation() throws Exception {\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n          .withPartitionAssignor(new IncompletePartitionAssignor())  // Mock assignor that drops partitions\n          .build();\n\n      String groupId = \"test-group\";\n      String memberId1 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n      String memberId2 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n      String topicName = \"test-topic\";\n      Uuid topicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n\n      // Create topic with 4 Analysis of the test files (`GroupCoordinatorServiceTest.java`, `GroupCoordinatorShardTest.java`, and `GroupMetadataManagerTest.java`) reveals several important failure modes and state transition scenarios that lack dedicated regression tests. These gaps expose the coordinator to potential data loss, incorrect partition assignments, resource leaks, and inconsistent group state transitions during error conditions.\n\n## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Member Epoch Transitions During Coordinator Unavailability\n\n- **Risk**: HIGH\n- **Code Location**: GroupCoordinatorService.java ~line 479-508 (consumerGroupHeartbeat method)\n- **Description**: When the coordinator is briefly unavailable (transitioning between leaders) and members continue sending heartbeats with incrementing epochs, the current tests only verify the COORDINATOR_NOT_AVAILABLE error response. However, there's no test ensuring that when the coordinator becomes available again, it correctly processes the accumulated epoch changes without skipping any transitions or duplicating assignments. This can lead to members being assigned to the same partition.\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testConsumerGroupHeartbeatEpochTransitionsAcrossCoordinatorFailover() throws ExecutionException, InterruptedException, TimeoutException {\n      GroupCoordinatorService service = new GroupCoordinatorServiceBuilder()\n          .setConfig(createConfig())\n          .setRuntime(mockRuntime())\n          .build();\n\n      String groupId = \"test-group\";\n      String memberId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n\n      // Service not started - coordinator unavailable\n      ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData request = new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .setMemberId(memberId)\n          .setMemberEpoch(0)\n          .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n          .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"topic-1\"))\n          .setTopicPartitions(List.of());\n\n      CompletableFuture<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData> future1 = service.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n          requestContext(ApiKeys.CONSUMER_GROUP_HEARTBEAT),\n          request\n      );\n\n      assertEquals(Errors.COORDINATOR_NOT_AVAILABLE.code(), future1.get(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS).errorCode());\n\n      // Start coordinator\n      service.start();\n\n      // Member sends heartbeat with epoch 1 (skipped epoch 0 transition)\n      request.setMemberEpoch(1);\n      CompletableFuture<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData> future2 = service.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n          requestContext(ApiKeys.CONSUMER_GROUP_HEARTBEAT),\n          request\n      );\n\n      // Verify the assignment contains this member (not another member)\n      ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData response = future2.get(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n      assertTrue(response.memberEpoch() >= 1, \"Member should have valid epoch after failover\");\n      assertNotEquals(Errors.FENCED_INSTANCE_ID.code(), response.errorCode());\n\n      service.shutdown();\n  }\n  ```\n- **Coverage Delta**: This test would exercise the `throwIfNotActive()` check at line 479, the state transition logic in GroupMetadataManager for member epoch validation, and the recovery path when the coordinator becomes active again. It hits critical paths in `GroupMetadataManager.consumerGroupHeartbeat()`.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Offset Expiration During Rebalance In Progress\n\n- **Risk**: HIGH\n- **Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java (offset expiration logic during group state transitions)\n- **Description**: Offsets can expire based on inactivity, but the existing tests (`GroupMetadataManagerTest`) don't verify that offset expiration is correctly skipped or handled when a group is in the REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS state. If offset expiration proceeds during rebalancing, committed offsets could be lost mid-rebalance, causing consumers to restart from the wrong position or lose progress entirely.\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testOffsetExpirationSkippedDuringRebalanceInProgress() throws Exception {\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n          .build();\n\n      String groupId = \"test-group\";\n      String memberId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n      String topicName = \"test-topic\";\n      Uuid topicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n\n      // Create consumer group and commit offsets\n      context.replay(\n          new ConsumerGroupMemberMetadataValue()\n              .setMemberId(memberId)\n              .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n      );\n\n      OffsetCommitRequestData offsetCommitRequest = new OffsetCommitRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .addTopic(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestTopic()\n              .setName(topicName)\n              .addPartition(new OffsetCommitRequestData.OffsetCommitRequestPartition()\n                  .setPartitionIndex(0)\n                  .setCommittedOffset(100)\n                  .setCommitTimestamp(context.time.milliseconds())\n              )\n          );\n\n      context.groupMetadataManager.commitOffset(requestContext(), offsetCommitRequest);\n\n      // Trigger rebalance - group state becomes REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS\n      ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData heartbeatRequest = new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .setMemberId(memberId)\n          .setMemberEpoch(0)\n          .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n          .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n          .setTopicPartitions(List.of());\n\n      context.groupMetadataManager.consumerGroupHeartbeat(requestContext(), heartbeatRequest);\n\n      // Advance time beyond offset retention\n      context.time.sleep(context.offsetsRetentionMs + 1000);\n\n      // Offset should still exist because group is rebalancing\n      OffsetFetchRequestData fetchRequest = new OffsetFetchRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .addTopic(new OffsetFetchRequestData.OffsetFetchRequestTopic()\n              .setName(topicName)\n              .addPartition(0)\n          );\n\n      OffsetFetchResponseData fetchResponse = context.groupMetadataManager.fetchOffsets(requestContext(), fetchRequest);\n      assertEquals(100L, fetchResponse.topics().get(0).partitions().get(0).committedOffset());\n\n      context.close();\n  }\n  ```\n- **Coverage Delta**: This test exercises offset expiration logic in OffsetMetadataManager while the group is in REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS state. It validates the state machine's protection against premature offset deletion and hits the isOffsetExpired check in OffsetMetadataManager that considers group state.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Member Removal with Unresolved Assignments\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java (member removal logic), GroupCoordinatorShard.java (deleteGroups method ~line 269)\n- **Description**: When a member is removed from a group (via LeaveGroup or timeout), the current test coverage doesn't verify that partial or in-flight partition assignments are correctly cleaned up. If a member's target assignment record exists but hasn't been applied (current assignment not yet updated), removing the member without cleaning up the target assignment can cause the partition to remain unassigned or cause conflicts when another member joins.\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testMemberRemovalWithPendingTargetAssignment() throws Exception {\n      // Member leaves before current assignment is applied\n      LeaveGroupRequestData leaveRequest = new LeaveGroupRequestData()\n          .setGroupId(groupId)\n          .addMember(new LeaveGroupRequestData.MemberIdentity()\n              .setMemberId(memberId1)\n          );\n\n      CoordinatorResult<LeaveGroupResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> leaveResult =\n GroupMetadataManager.leaveGroup() and validates cleanup of both current and target assignments. It hits the record generation logic that creates tombstone records for ConsumerGroupTargetAssignmentMemberValue.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Concurrent Offset Commits During Member Epoch Bump\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java (offset commit validation), OffsetMetadataManager.java (commitOffset method)\n- **Description**: When a member's epoch is bumped during rebalancing, a consumer might simultaneously attempt to commit offsets using its old epoch. The current tests don't verify that offset commits from members with outdated epochs are correctly rejected with FENCED_MEMBER_EPOCH, preventing the coordinator from accepting stale offsets. This can result in incorrect offset tracking if a consumer commits with a stale epoch before realizing it has been fenced.\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n          .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n          .setTopicPartitions(List.of());\n\n      CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, .setMemberId(memberId)\n          .setMemberEpoch(firstEpoch)\n          .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n          .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n          .setTopicPartitions(List.of());\n\n      CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> rebalanceResult =\n
